          "description": "Log divergence AND show a warning banner on the dashboard so it's visible immediately. Still non-blocking."
        },
        {
          "label": "Log only",
          "description": "Silent logging to the comparison file. No dashboard notification — review happens post-run by checking the files."
        }
      ],
      "multiSelect": false
    }
  ]
}

          "label": "Migration window only",
          "description": "Zod preprocess handles old format during parallel validation (3 runs). After cutover, remove old-format parsing — progress file is new-format only. Simpler long-term."
        },
        {
          "label": "Permanent dual-format",
          "description": "Keep Zod preprocess transforms forever. If someone manually edits the progress file or rolls back, old format still works. Defensive but adds permanent complexity."
        },
        {
          "label": "You decide",
          "description": "Claude chooses based on what the Zod schemas already support from Phase 15."
        }
      ],
      "multiSelect": false
    }
  ]
}
```

**Output:** ```
User has answered your questions: "Should the progress file reader support old-format files permanently, or only during a migration window?"="Migration window only". You can now continue with the user's answers in mind.
